[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m def strategy(board):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m     def possible_moves(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m         moves = []
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m         for i in range(len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m             for j in range(len(board[i])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                 if board[i][j] == 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                     moves.append("W" if i > 0 else "A" if j > 0 else "S" if i < len(board) - 1 else "D")

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m     def apply_move(board, move):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m         if move == "W":
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m             return [list(x) for x in zip(*board[::-1])]

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m     best_move = possible_moves(board)[weigh.index(max(weigh))]

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m def move(board, direction):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m         for col in range(len(board[0])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             values = [board[row][col] for row in range(len(board)) if board[row][col] != 0]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             merged = merge(values)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             for row in range(len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m                 board[row][col] = merged[row] if row < len(merged) else 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m     elif direction == "A":
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m         for row in range(len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             values = [board[row][col] for col in range(len(board[0])) if board[row][col] != 0]

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             for col in range(len(board[0])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m                 board[row][col] = merged[col] if col < len(merged) else 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m     elif direction == "S":
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m         for col in range(len(board[0])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             values = [board[row][col] for row in range(len(board) - 1, -1, -1) if board[row][col] != 0][::-1]

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             merged = merge(values)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             for col in range(len(board[0]) - 1, -1, -1):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m def merge(values):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m     merged = []
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m     for value in values:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m         if not merged or merged[-1] != value:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             merged.append(value)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m         else:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m             merged[-1] *= 2
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m     while len(merged) < len(values):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m         merged.append(0)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479147)[0m     return merged

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m     def is_valid_move(board, direction):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m         dx, dy = dirs[direction] * 1, dirs[direction] * -1

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m             # Move all non-zero tiles to the left
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m             result = []

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m                     result.append(tile)

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m         
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m         def merge(row):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m             # Merge adjacent tiles with the same value

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479149)[0m             for i in range(len(row) - 1):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m def strategy(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     """
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     A simple strategy for playing the 2048 game. 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     This function checks if any moves (`W`, `A`, `S`, `D`) would result in a board that
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     maximizes the highest number on the board after the move. If multiple moves result in
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     the same highest number, it will choose the move that brings the number to the top-left corner

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                 while 0 in row:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                     row.remove(0)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                 for j in range(1, len(row)):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m         for i in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m             for j in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                 if board[i][j] % 2 == 0 and board[i][j] != 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                     scores[direction] += 2 ** (board[i][j] - 1)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                 elif board[i][j] % 2 == 1 and board[i][j] != 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m                     scores[direction] += 2 ** (board[i][j] - 2)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m     # Bump towards the highest number but try merge if possible
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m     best_move = max(scores, key=scores.get)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m     if scores[best_move] == 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m         best_move = 'A'  # Fall back to left if no good merge
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m     return best_move
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479148)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m [2048] sample 81 | steps=0 state=timeout score=1.0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m def strategy(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     empty_cells = [(i, j) for i in range(4) for j in range(4) if board[i][j] == 0]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     if empty_cells:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         return "W"  # Move up
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     max_tile = max([max(row) for row in board])
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     # Check for possible moves

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     if can_move_left:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         return "A"
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     elif can_move_right:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         return "D"
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     elif can_move_down:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         return "S"
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     else:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         return "A"  # Fallback move if no better option

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     """

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     def can_move(direction):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         if direction == 'W':
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m             for row in range(1, len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                 for col in range(len(board[row])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                     if board[row][col] != 0 and board[row][col] == board[row-1][col]:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                         return True
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         elif direction == 'A':
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m             for col in range(1, len(board[0])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                 for row in range(len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                     if board[row][col] != 0 and board[row][col] == board[row][col-1]:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                         return True
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         elif direction == 'S':
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m             for row in range(len(board)-2, -1, -1):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                 for col in range(len(board[row])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                     if board[row][col] != 0 and board[row][col] == board[row+1][col]:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                         return True

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                 for row in range(len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                     if board[row][col] != 0 and board[row][col] == board[row][col+1]:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m                         return True
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         return False
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     for direction in ['W', 'A', 'S', 'D']:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m         if can_move(direction):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m             return direction
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479143)[0m     return "A"  # Default if no moves are possible

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m [2048] sample 59 | steps=0 state=timeout score=1.0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m def strategy(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     # Check for the presence of any 2's or 4's as they are safer to merge
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     safe_merge = any(2 in row or 4 in row for row in board) or any(2 in col or 4 in col for col in zip(*board))
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     # Heuristic: Count number of zero values and their position
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     zeros = [i for i, row in enumerate(board) for j, val in enumerate(row) if val == 0]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     zero_count = len(zeros)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     zero_positions = zeros
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     # If there are zeros, move to a position with adjacent zeros
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     if zero_count > 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         if zero_positions:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             x, y = zero_positions[0] // len(board[0]), zero_positions[0] % len(board[0])
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if x > 0 and board[x-1][y] == 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'W'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if y > 0 and board[x][y-1] == 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'A'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if x < len(board) - 1 and board[x+1][y] == 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'S'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if y < len(board[0]) - 1 and board[x][y+1] == 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'D'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     # Otherwise, if there's a safe merge, move towards it
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     if safe_merge:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         for i in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if i == 0 and not any(row[0] == 2 or row[0] == 4 for row in board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'L'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if i == 1 and not any(row[len(row)-1] == 2 or row[len(row)-1] == 4 for row in board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'R'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if i == 2 and not any(col[0] == 2 or col[0] == 4 for col in zip(*board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'U'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m             if i == 3 and not any(col[len(col)-1] == 2 or col[len(col)-1] == 4 for col in zip(*board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 return 'D'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     # Otherwise, move towards the highest numbered tile to avoid collisions
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     max_val = max(max(row) for row in board)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     max_positions = [(i, j) for i, row in enumerate(board) for j, val in enumerate(row) if val == max_val]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     x, y = max_positions[0]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     if x > 0 and board[x-1][y] != 0 and board[x-1][y] != max_val:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'W'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     if y > 0 and board[x][y-1] != 0 and board[x][y-1] != max_val:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'A'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     if x < len(board) - 1 and board[x+1][y] != 0 and board[x+1][y] != max_val:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'S'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     if y < len(board[0]) - 1 and board[x][y+1] != 0 and board[x][y+1] != max_val:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'D'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     # Default to the direction providing the most zeros
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     zero_counts = {'U': 0, 'D': 0, 'L': 0, 'R': 0}
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     for i in range(len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         zero_counts['U'] += board[0].count(0)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         zero_counts['D'] += board[-1].count(0)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         zero_counts['L'] += sum(row[0] == 0 for row in board)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         zero_counts['R'] += sum(row[-1] == 0 for row in board)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     if zero_counts['U'] > 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'U'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     elif zero_counts['D'] > 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'D'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     elif zero_counts['L'] > 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'L'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m     else:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m         return 'R'
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     def calculate_probabilities(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         probabilities = {"W": 0, "A": 0, "S": 0, "D": 0}
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         empty_cells = [(i, j) for i in range(len(board)) for j in range(len(board[0])) if board[i][j] == 0]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         for move, new_board in zip("WASD", [move_up(board), move_left(board), move_down(board), move_right(board)]):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             if new_board != board:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 moved_cells = [(i, j) for i in range(len(board)) for j in range(len(board[0])) if board[i][j] != new_board[i][j]]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 probabilities[move] = len(empty_cells) * 0.05 + len(moved_cells) * 0.45
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             else:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 probabilities[move] = 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         if not empty_cells:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             best_move = max(probabilities, key=probabilities.get)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             remaining_prob = 1 - probabilities[best_move]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             probabilities = {k: v * remaining_prob / 3 for k, v in probabilities.items() if k != best_move}
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             probabilities[best_move] = 1 - sum(probabilities.values())
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         return probabilities
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     def move_up(board):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         for j in range(len(board[0])):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             column = [new_board[i][j] for i in range(len(board))]

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             for element in column:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 if element != 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     new_board[index][j] = element
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     if index != column.index(element):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                         new_board[column.index(element)][j] = 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     index += 1
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             for k in range(index, len(board)):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 new_board[k][j] = 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         return new_board
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     probabilities = calculate_probabilities(board)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     max_probability = max(probabilities.values())
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     best_moves = [move for move, prob in probabilities.items() if prob == max_probability]

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     empty = [-1, -1]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     def find_empty(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         for r in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             for c in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 if board[r][c] == 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     return (r, c)

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     def is_full(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         for row in board:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             if 0 in row:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 return False
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         return True
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     def move_up(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         for c in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             stack = []
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             for r in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 if board[r][c] != 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     if stack and stack[-1] == board[r][c]:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                         stack[-1] *= 2
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     else:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                         stack.append(board[r][c])
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             for r in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 board[r][c] = stack[r] if r < len(stack) else 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         return board
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m 
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m     def move_down(board):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m         for c in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             stack = []
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             for r in range(3, -1, -1):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                 if board[r][c] != 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     if stack and stack[-1] == board[r][c]:

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m                     else:

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479142)[0m             for r in range(3, -1, -1):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m def strategy(board):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                 if downValue > maxDownValue:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m                     maxDownValue = downValue

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=479144)[0m
